<div id="review_1752134774" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1752134774" />
    <a title="Ashley Marie " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29787548-ashley-marie"><img alt="Ashley Marie " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1471208025p2/29787548.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1752134774?book_show_action=true">Oct 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ashley Marie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ashley Marie " href="/user/show/29787548-ashley-marie">Ashley Marie </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29787548-ashley-marie?shelf=histfic-alt-history">histfic-alt-history</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29787548-ashley-marie?shelf=fantasy-paranormal">fantasy-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29787548-ashley-marie?shelf=steampunk">steampunk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29787548-ashley-marie?shelf=audiobook-would-recommend">audiobook-would-recommend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29787548-ashley-marie?shelf=kickass-ladies">kickass-ladies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29787548-ashley-marie?shelf=absurdist-whimsy-escapism">absurdist-whimsy-escapism</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29787548-ashley-marie?shelf=lgbtqiap">lgbtqiap</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1752134774" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1914799748511343741">For all the pronunciation differences between this and the Finishing School books, I still enjoyed the audio immensely. Emily Gray did a fantastic job and I'm dying for book three, not in the least thanks to that ending. "What could happen in the final 5-10 minutes?" Ohhhh buddy. I won't be asking that question again when it comes to Gail Carriger's books. Wuff.<br/><br/>I loved the inclusion of Sidheag Maccon and Genevieve Lefoux, two of my Finishing School favorites. The timelines get a bit mixed up in </span>
  <span id="freeText1914799748511343741" style="display:none">For all the pronunciation differences between this and the Finishing School books, I still enjoyed the audio immensely. Emily Gray did a fantastic job and I'm dying for book three, not in the least thanks to that ending. "What could happen in the final 5-10 minutes?" Ohhhh buddy. I won't be asking that question again when it comes to Gail Carriger's books. Wuff.<br /><br />I loved the inclusion of Sidheag Maccon and Genevieve Lefoux, two of my Finishing School favorites. The timelines get a bit mixed up in my head to the point where I wonder if I shouldn't have read this series first and then gone back and read the prequel series, considering publication order... but I don't care, I like it this way :)<br /><br /><b>BR with a select few awesome MacHalos</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer68261189733978052">4.5 STARS read<br/><br/>I must admit I thought book 1 was good but that's about it. On the other hand, book 2 was AMAZING, loved every page of it!   <span id="freeText68261189733978052" style="display:none">4.5 STARS read<br /><br />I must admit I thought book 1 was good but that's about it. On the other hand, book 2 was AMAZING, loved every page of it! It took me a while to get into the book because the topic is so very different from everything else, but once I did I could not put it down. <br /><br />I'll explain a bit for those who have not read it yet. We have this amazing soulless Italian heroine who is very practical and efficient, then we have her super sexy alpha werewolf of a husband. Both of them make such a great couple, I love every moment they spend together. I'll say I just can't get enough of them. Alexia has a special power, every time she touches a supernatural being they turn human while she keeps touching them. And her power is not common at all. So most people just want her dead. She also has a very hilarious vampire fond of young fellows as her best friend who I love to read about. But the best is the way the author writes, very English. Great sense of humor.<br /><br />Now here's something you all need to know: CLIFF HANGER ALERT! I usually hate them, but as book 3 is already out this did not turn into a problem IMHO, but only made the series more appealing as I cold do nothing else until I read the beginning of book 3.<br /><br />I must admit I am a huge fan of this series now and I can't put it down. Can't wait to read next book. Although if next book is not as good or better, I'll probably be extremely disappointed. </span>

  <span id="freeText685756671108126419" style="display:none">For some reason the first half of the book didn't hold my attention very well. I'd read four or five pages and then set it down. An hour later, I'd pick it up and try again. Maybe I just wasn't in the right kind of mood...<br />At any rate, halfway through the story things picked up (either my mood changed or the plot got better), and I pretty much finished the rest of it in one sitting. I guess what I'm trying to say is that this one is definitely worth finishing.<br />Also, I had read some of the other reviewers' comments about the 'big shock' at the end of the book, so I thought I was pretty prepared for whatever was coming down the line. I was really wrong. Even thought I knew something was going to happen, my mouth was still gaping open when I closed the book. I have to admit, I never saw that one coming.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CRPgozbRJnh3YtpSgXQ1Iq+x4CekjY3g6FPU5HG12c9QBOwJT60DU6novtSmY0wIib16YzESIDTp9iOAaUriYA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2GZkV/UIgEyX/2qpqmnv28uCPB36SFnfl/RMvBZfNieBcWj9jHSlZ0l1Di+Nfpbx7Y6mWW/X9AuWUbvYDqANiA==')})
  }
